    function create_ezolpl() {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));
     var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
     __ez.ck.setByCat("ezux_lpl_2228=" + new Date().getTime() + "|fde6a8c8-f532-4f63-4011-efce2b59a46f; " + expires, 3);
 }
 function attach_ezolpl() {
     if(window.attachEvent) {
         window.attachEvent('onload', create_ezolpl);
     } else {
         if(window.onload) {
             var curronload = window.onload;
             var newonload = function(evt) {
                 curronload(evt);
                 create_ezolpl();
             };
             window.onload = newonload;
         } else {
             window.onload = create_ezolpl;
         }
     }
 }

    function ez_isclean( data ) {
     if (typeof data === 'undefined') { data = document.URL; }
     var re = /(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))(@|%2540|%40)((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))/;
     var isClean = !re.test(data);
     return isClean;
 }
 
 var ez_queue = new Array();
 function sort_queue(a, b)
 {
   if( a.priority < b.priority ) return -1;
   else if( a.priority == b.priority ) return 0;
   else return 1;
 }
 function execute_ez_queue()
 {
   ez_queue.sort( sort_queue );
 
   for( var i in ez_queue )
   {
         if(typeof ez_queue[i].method != "undefined")
         {
             try{
                 ez_queue[i].method.call( null );
             }
             catch (err) {
 
             }
         }
   }
 }
 
 window.ez_ad_units = new Array();
 window.ezslots = new Array();
 function ez_write_tag(d) {
     if(ez_isclean() && d instanceof Array) {
 
 		ez_ad_units[ez_ad_units.length] = d;
         var ezcmd = "googletag.cmd.push(function() {var divid = 'div-gpt-ad-"+d[1]+"-0';if(typeof ezlrarn == 'function'){ezlrarn(divid);}googletag.display(divid);var to = 0;if("+d[2]+".getTargeting('ga')[0] == '0'){to = 500;console.log('"+d[2]+" - no google');}if(window.ezDisableInitialLoad==true){setTimeout(function(){googletag.pubads().refresh(["+d[2]+"])},to);}});";
 		return ezcmd;
     }
     else {
         return "1+1";
     }
 }
 function in_array(needle, haystack) {
     var length = haystack.length;
     for(var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
         if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
     }
     return false;
 }

            <font cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:99px;wocalc:99px;hcalc:60px;rend_px_area:0;" size="+2" style="font-size:24px;nodepath:/html/body/center[1]/p/font;pagepos:11;cwidth:99;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:99px;wocalc:99px;hcalc:60;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:98;req_px_area:9266.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:31.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
             Welcome to the

           <img alt="Constitution Society" cwidth="525" data-orig-height="60" data-orig-width="525" eza="cwidth:525px;;cheight:60px;;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:525px;wocalc:525px;hcalc:60px;rend_px_area:31500;" src="img/con_soc.gif" style="width:525px;height:60px;nodepath:/html/body/center[1]/img;pagepos:12;cwidth:525px;cheight:60px;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:525px;wocalc:525px;hcalc:60;rend_px_area:31500;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:0;obj_px_area:31500;req_px_area:31500;req_px_height:0;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;"/>

          <p cwidth="1185" eza="cwidth:1185px;;cheight:42px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:94px;wocalc:94px;hcalc:441px;rend_px_area:49770;" style="nodepath:/html/body/p[1];pagepos:13;cwidth:1185px;cheight:42px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:94px;hcalc:441;rend_px_area:49770;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:131;req_px_area:52258.5;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
           This site aims to eventually provide almost everything one needs
       to accurately decide what is and is not constitutional in most
       situations, and what applicable constitutions require one to do.
       It is for constitutional decision support.
          </p>
          <!--scale from memcache - scale-c288a2188c92c2cc496ba8835004ab8c-1.000-10-0-782aea2347c393187dfaa3cc44d88ebe-750-170-1-0-176-6-mod14 -->

          <p cwidth="1185" eza="cwidth:1185px;;cheight:42px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:483px;rend_px_area:49770;" style="nodepath:/html/body/p[2];pagepos:14;cwidth:1185px;cheight:42px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:483;rend_px_area:49770;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:131;req_px_area:52258.5;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
           The Constitution Society is a private non-profit organization
       dedicated to research and public education on the principles of
       constitutional republican government. It publishes documentation,
       engages in litigation, and organizes local citizens groups to work
       for reform.
          </p>
          <!--scale from memcache - scale-e20f89c8d3c3a20b592b7314e7916974-1.000-10-0-782aea2347c393187dfaa3cc44d88ebe-750-170-1-0-176-6-mod14 -->

          <p cwidth="1185" eza="cwidth:1185px;;cheight:105px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:1365px;rend_px_area:124425;" style="nodepath:/html/body/p[3];pagepos:15;cwidth:1185px;cheight:105px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:200px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:1365;rend_px_area:124425;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:131;req_px_area:130646.25;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
           <span class="ezoic-ad medrectangle-3" data-ez-name="constitution_org-medrectangle-3" style="display:inline-block;float:left;margin-bottom:4px !important;margin-left:1px !important;margin-right:28px !important;margin-top:2px !important;min-height:110px;min-width:728px;">
            <span class="ezoic-ad" ezah="90" ezaw="728" id="div-gpt-ad-constitution_org-medrectangle-3-0" style="position:relative;z-index:501;display:inline-block;">
             <script data-cfasync="false" style="display:none;" type="text/javascript">
              eval(ez_write_tag([[728,90],'constitution_org-medrectangle-3','ezslot_0']));
             </script>
            </span>
           </span>
           This organization was founded in response to the growing concern
       that noncompliance with the Constitution for the United States of
       America and most state constitutions is creating a crisis of
       legitimacy that threatens freedom and civil rights. Although the
       focus here is on government in the United States, coverage also
       includes the rest of the world, and private as well as public
       organizations. We maintain that the principles of constitutional
       republicanism are universal, and applicable to all nations,
       although not well understood or upheld by most. We also examine
       the related principles of federalism and nomocracy, the rule of
       law, of nomology, the science of law, and show how those
       principles are applicable to solving the fundamental problem of
       avoiding excessive or unbalanced concentrations of power.
          </p>
